# [`clinvar`](https://bioregistry.io/clinvar): ClinVar Variation

This page summarize the different resources that reference `clinvar`
but use local unique identifiers that do not match the standard pattern of
`^\d+$`. Of the 2 resources,
1 variants on the standard prefix were found: ['ClinVar'].

## `orphanet`: Orphanet

Identifiers for this prefix are given incorrectly in `orphanet`.
